Repeated Test¶

K-Means++¶

In [13]:
kmeanspp = {
    'silhouette': [],
    'sse' : [],
    'quantization' : [],
}
for _ in range(20):
    kmean_rep = KMeans(n_cluster=3, init_pp=True)
    kmean_rep.fit(x)
    predicted_kmean_rep = kmean_rep.predict(x)
    silhouette = silhouette_score(x, predicted_kmean_rep)
    sse = kmean_rep.SSE
    quantization = quantization_error(centroids=kmean_rep.centroid, data=x, labels=predicted_kmean_rep)
    kmeanspp['silhouette'].append(silhouette)
    kmeanspp['sse'].append(sse)
    kmeanspp['quantization'].append(quantization)

PSO¶

In [14]:
%%time
pso_plain = {
    'silhouette': [],
    'sse' : [],
    'quantization' : [],
}
for _ in range(20):
    pso_rep = ParticleSwarmOptimizedClustering(
        n_cluster=3, n_particles=10, data=x, hybrid=False, max_iter=2000, print_debug=2000)
    pso_rep.run()
    pso_kmeans = KMeans(n_cluster=3, init_pp=False, seed=2018)
    pso_kmeans.centroid = pso_rep.gbest_centroids.copy()
    predicted_pso_rep = pso_kmeans.predict(x)
    
    silhouette = silhouette_score(x, predicted_pso_rep)
    sse = calc_sse(centroids=pso_rep.gbest_centroids, data=x, labels=predicted_pso_rep)
    quantization = pso_rep.gbest_score
    pso_plain['silhouette'].append(silhouette)
    pso_plain['sse'].append(sse)
    pso_plain['quantization'].append(quantization)

PSO Hybrid¶

In [15]:
%%time
pso_hybrid = {
    'silhouette': [],
    'sse' : [],
    'quantization' : [],
}
for _ in range(20):
    pso_rep = ParticleSwarmOptimizedClustering(
        n_cluster=3, n_particles=10, data=x, hybrid=True, max_iter=2000, print_debug=2000)
    pso_rep.run()
    pso_kmeans = KMeans(n_cluster=3, init_pp=False, seed=2018)
    pso_kmeans.centroid = pso_rep.gbest_centroids.copy()
    predicted_pso_rep = pso_kmeans.predict(x)
    
    silhouette = silhouette_score(x, predicted_pso_rep)
    sse = calc_sse(centroids=pso_rep.gbest_centroids, data=x, labels=predicted_pso_rep)
    quantization = pso_rep.gbest_score
    pso_hybrid['silhouette'].append(silhouette)
    pso_hybrid['sse'].append(sse)
    pso_hybrid['quantization'].append(quantization)

obj_fun = ObjectiveFunction()
num_processes = cpu_count()  # number of logical CPUs
num_iterations = num_processes * 5  # each process does 5 iterations
results = harmony_search(obj_fun, num_processes, num_iterations)

from matplotlib import pyplot as plt
sse_mean = [22.02436308, 27.08025074, 22.0707652, 25.06040326]
sse_stdev = [0, 7.395153008, 0.016732686, 5.423698526]
silhouette_mean = [0.422105257, 0.395904088, 0.422126762, 0.412854659]
silhouette_stdev = [0, 0.040273107, 0, 0]
quantization_mean = [0.301664619, 0.320625773, 0.301247072, 0.321652545]
quantization_stdev = [0, 0.011036628, 0.000147039, 0.012078442]
index = ['K-Means++','PSO','PSO Hybrid','HSA']
df = pd.DataFrame({'sse_mean' : sse_mean,'sse_stdev' : sse_stdev,'silhouette_mean' : silhouette_mean,'silhouette_stdev' : silhouette_stdev,'quantization_mean' : quantization_mean,'quantization_stdev' : quantization_stdev}, index=index)
ax = df.plot.bar(rot=0,stacked=True)
plt.title("Benchmark between K-Means++,PSO,PSO Hybrid,HSA")
plt.xlabel("Method")
plt.ylabel("Standards")
plt.rcParams["figure.figsize"] = [20,15]
